# Task: Debug Query Plan Regression in TiDB Cost-Based Optimizer

## Background
A user reports that after upgrading TiDB, a query that previously used an index scan is now doing a full table scan. The query involves a JOIN between two tables with a WHERE clause on an indexed column.

## Objective
Investigate the cost model in TiDB's query optimizer to identify which component could cause a plan regression where an IndexScan is replaced by a TableFullScan.

## Steps
1. Find the cost model implementation in `pkg/planner/core/` that computes the cost of IndexScan vs TableFullScan
2. Identify the `Stats` struct and how row count estimates feed into the cost calculation
3. Locate where the optimizer compares candidate plans and selects the cheapest
4. Create a file `debug_report.md` in `/workspace/` documenting:
   - The file paths and functions responsible for cost calculation of IndexScan
   - The file paths and functions responsible for cost calculation of TableFullScan
   - The comparison logic that picks the final plan
   - A hypothesis for what parameter change could cause the regression

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/planner/core/` — optimizer core
- `pkg/planner/cardinality/` — cardinality estimation
- `pkg/statistics/` — statistics framework

## Success Criteria
- debug_report.md exists and contains the relevant file paths
- Report identifies cost model functions for both scan types
- Report includes a plausible regression hypothesis

61-assistanttext-
`/workspace/debug_report.md` has been created. Here's a summary of the findings:

## Key Findings

### IndexScan Cost Functions
- **Ver1:** `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer1` — `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go:425`
  Formula: `rowCount × rowSize × scanFactor`
- **Ver2:** `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer2` — `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go:123`
  Formula: `rows × log2(rowSize) × scanFactor`

### TableFullScan Cost Functions
- **Ver1:** `(*PhysicalTableScan).GetPlanCostVer1` — `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go:400`
  Same formula, but `rowSize` covers all table columns (wider than index columns)
- **Ver2:** `(*PhysicalTableScan).GetPlanCostVer2` — `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go:140`
  Same log2 formula, plus optional `PreferRangeScan` penalty for unreliable stats

### Plan Comparison Logic
- `skylinePruning` (`find_best_task.go:1119`) does a pre-cost filter on non-cost dimensions
- `compareTaskCost` (`find_best_task.go:349`) does the final cost comparison: `curCost < bestCost`
- `getPlanCost` (`plan_cost_ver2.go:46`) dispatches between Ver1 and Ver2 based on `tidb_cost_model_version`

### Regression Hypothesis
The most likely cause is the **upgrade from cost model Ver1 to Ver2** (default changed in v6.5). Ver2 uses `log2(rowSize)` instead of `rowSize`, which compresses the cost advantage of IndexScan for wide-row tables — when combined with stale index histograms (high `ModifyCount` relative to `RealtimeCount`), this inflates the IndexScan's row count estimate enough to tip the optimizer toward TableFullScan.

  "content": "# TiDB Cost-Based Optimizer: IndexScan vs TableFullScan Regression Analysis\n\n## Overview\n\nThis report documents the cost model components in TiDB's query optimizer that govern\nthe choice between IndexScan and TableFullScan, and identifies how a parameter change\ncould cause a plan regression.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Cost Calculation for IndexScan\n\n### Cost Model Version 1 (Ver1)\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go`  \n**Function:** `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer1` (line 425)\n\nFormula:\n```\nselfCost = rowCount * rowSize * scanFactor\n```\n\n- `rowCount` \u2014 from `getCardinality(p, costFlag)`, which reads `p.StatsInfo().RowCount`\n- `rowSize` \u2014 from `p.getScanRowSize()`, i.e., average byte size of projected index columns\n- `scanFactor` \u2014 from `sessVars.GetScanFactor(p.Table)` (session var `tidb_opt_scan_factor`, default 1.5);\n  switches to `GetDescScanFactor` for descending scans larger than `cost.SmallScanThreshold` (10 000 rows)\n\n### Cost Model Version 2 (Ver2)\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go`  \n**Function:** `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer2` (line 123)\n\nFormula (via `scanCostVer2`):\n```\ncost = rows * max(log2(rowSize), 0) * scanFactor\n```\n\n- `rows` \u2014 `getCardinality(p, option.CostFlag)`\n- `rowSize` \u2014 `getAvgRowSize(p.StatsInfo(), p.schema.Columns)` (index columns only)\n- `scanFactor` \u2014 from `getTaskScanFactorVer2(p, kv.TiKV, taskType)`\n\nHelper: `scanCostVer2` (line 841) \u2014 enforces `rowSize >= 1` before applying log2.\n\nThe `IndexReader` wrapper adds a **network cost** on top:\n```\nnetCost = rows * rowSize * netFactor\nplanCost = (childCost + netCost) / distConcurrency\n```\n(`PhysicalIndexReader.GetPlanCostVer2`, line 216)\n\n---\n\n## 2. Cost Calculation for TableFullScan\n\n### Cost Model Version 1 (Ver1)\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go`  \n**Function:** `(*PhysicalTableScan).GetPlanCostVer1` (line 400)\n\nFormula (identical structure to IndexScan Ver1):\n```\nselfCost = rowCount * rowSize * scanFactor\n```\n\n- `rowCount` \u2014 cardinality estimate for the table scan (usually the full table row count when no predicates narrow the range)\n- `rowSize` \u2014 `p.getScanRowSize()`, but for a table scan this includes **all projected table columns**, which is generally wider than an index's columns\n- `scanFactor` \u2014 same `GetScanFactor` / `GetDescScanFactor` as IndexScan\n\n### Cost Model Version 2 (Ver2)\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go`  \n**Function:** `(*PhysicalTableScan).GetPlanCostVer2` (line 140)\n\nFormula (via `scanCostVer2`):\n```\ncost = rows * log2(rowSize) * scanFactor\n```\n\nNotable differences from IndexScan Ver2:\n\n1. **Minimum row/size guard** (`MinNumRows = 1.0`, `MinRowSize = 2.0`) is applied when the\n   scan is NOT a child of an IndexLookUp (lines 154\u2013157). This prevents underestimation of\n   standalone full-table scans.\n\n2. **TiFlash startup penalty** (`TiFlashStartupRowPenalty = 10 000` rows, line 164) is added\n   when the store type is TiFlash, to bias small scans toward TiKV.\n\n3. **PreferRangeScan penalty** (lines 165\u2013191): when `tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan` is on AND\n   the table stats are unreliable (`Pseudo`, zero `RealtimeCount`, high `ModifyCount`, or low\n   estimate), an additional cost equal to `max(1000, ModifyCount, RealtimeCount) * rowSize *\n   scanFactor` is added to discourage full table scans.\n\nThe `TableReader` wrapper adds:\n```\nnetCost = rows * rowSize * netFactor\nplanCost = (childCost + netCost) / distConcurrency\n```\n(`PhysicalTableReader.GetPlanCostVer2`, line 241)\n\n---\n\n## 3. Plan Comparison Logic\n\n### Skyline Pruning (pre-cost filter)\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go`  \n**Function:** `skylinePruning` (line 1119)\n\nBefore cost is computed, `skylinePruning` eliminates dominated access paths by comparing\ncandidates on multiple non-cost dimensions (number of access conditions, covering index,\nsort order compatibility, etc.).  Index paths are only considered if they have access\nconditions, match the required sort property, are forced, or provide a covering scan\n(`IsSingleScan`).  If none of those hold, the index candidate is skipped at line 1146.\n\nAfter pruning, the `preferRange` flag (line 1175) can discard full-scan candidates entirely\nwhen stats are pseudo or the table has no rows \u2014 even before cost comparison.\n\n### Per-DataSource Task Enumeration\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go`  \n**Function:** `findBestTask4DataSource` (called internally, lines 1377\u20131591)\n\nFor each surviving candidate:\n- Table paths \u2192 `convertToTableScan` (line 1539)\n- Index paths \u2192 `convertToIndexScan` (line 1569)\n\nEach resulting task is compared with `compareTaskCost` (line 1549 / 1578).\n\n### Cost Comparison\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go`  \n**Function:** `compareTaskCost` (line 349)\n\n```go\nfunc compareTaskCost(curTask, bestTask base.Task, ...) (curIsBetter bool, err error) {\n    curCost, ...  := getTaskPlanCost(curTask, ...)\n    bestCost, ... := getTaskPlanCost(bestTask, ...)\n    return curCost < bestCost, nil\n}\n```\n\n`getTaskPlanCost` (line 370) dispatches to `getPlanCost`, which selects **Ver1** or **Ver2**\nbased on `CostModelVersion == modelVer2` (`plan_cost_ver2.go:47`).\n\n### Top-level Enumeration\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go`  \n**Functions:** `findBestTask` (line 501), `enumeratePhysicalPlans4Task` (line 172)\n\nThe winner from `enumeratePhysicalPlans4Task` is stored via `p.StoreTask(prop, bestTask)`\nand is the plan that the optimizer commits to.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Regression Hypothesis\n\n### Most Likely Cause: Inflated Row-Count Estimate for IndexScan\n\nThe cost formula for both scan types is:\n\n```\ncost \u221d rowCount \u00d7 rowSize \u00d7 scanFactor\n```\n\nAn IndexScan becomes MORE expensive than a TableFullScan when its estimated `rowCount`\nis overestimated relative to the table scan's row count.\n\n**Concrete scenario \u2014 stale/missing index statistics:**\n\n1. A table is analyzed, but afterward a large batch INSERT/DELETE runs without a subsequent\n   `ANALYZE`. `ModifyCount` grows while `RealtimeCount` stays at the old value.\n\n2. When the optimizer estimates rows for `IndexScan` via `GetRowCountByIndexRanges`, the\n   index histogram is stale. Because `histColl.Pseudo` becomes `true` (or\n   `IndexStatsIsInvalid` returns true), the cardinality estimation falls back to\n   `RealtimeCount \u00d7 selectivity_factor`, which can be very large.\n\n3. Meanwhile, the **TableFullScan** row count is also re-estimated from `RealtimeCount`, but\n   for a full-range scan this is essentially the entire table \u2014 no worse than the index\n   estimate above.\n\n4. Under Ver2's `PreferRangeScan` penalty, the full-scan cost gets an **additional** penalty,\n   but if `tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan` is OFF (the default), this guard is absent and the\n   inflated index row count makes the IndexScan look more expensive.\n\n**Parameter that most directly controls the regression:**\n\n| Parameter | Effect |\n|---|---|\n| `tidb_opt_scan_factor` (`GetScanFactor`) | Multiplier applied equally to both scan types; increasing it cannot by itself cause a plan flip, but it amplifies any existing rowCount difference |\n| `tidb_cost_model_version` (1 \u2192 2) | Ver2 uses `log2(rowSize)` instead of `rowSize`; this changes the relative weight of wide vs narrow rows, potentially making full-table scans (wide rows) appear cheaper when the index row count is overestimated |\n| `tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan` | When OFF and index stats are stale, removes the penalty on TableFullScan that would otherwise compensate for underestimation |\n| Stale `HistColl` after bulk DML | Causes `IndexStatsIsInvalid \u2192 true`, reverting index selectivity to pseudo estimates and inflating IndexScan's row count estimate |\n\n**Most actionable hypothesis:**  \nAn upgrade that switched `tidb_cost_model_version` from 1 to 2 (default changed in TiDB v6.5)\nchanged the scan cost formula from `rows \u00d7 rowSize \u00d7 factor` to `rows \u00d7 log2(rowSize) \u00d7 factor`.\nFor tables with **wide rows** (large `rowSize`), `log2(rowSize)` is relatively smaller than\n`rowSize`, which compresses the difference between IndexScan and TableFullScan costs. If the\nindex's column set is also wide (e.g., a composite index covering many columns), its\n`log2(rowSize)` approaches that of the table scan, erasing the cost advantage of the index\nand causing the optimizer to prefer the full scan.\n\n**How to verify:** Run `EXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose'` and compare `estCost` values. Then check\n`SHOW STATS_META WHERE table_name = '...'` for high `modify_count` relative to `row_count`,\nand run `ANALYZE TABLE` to refresh statistics.\n\n---\n\n## Summary of Key Files\n\n| Concern | File | Function / Line |\n|---|---|---|\n| IndexScan cost (Ver1) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` | `GetPlanCostVer1` (PhysicalIndexScan), line 425 |\n| TableFullScan cost (Ver1) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` | `GetPlanCostVer1` (PhysicalTableScan), line 400 |\n| IndexScan cost (Ver2) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | `GetPlanCostVer2` (PhysicalIndexScan), line 123 |\n| TableFullScan cost (Ver2) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | `GetPlanCostVer2` (PhysicalTableScan), line 140 |\n| Scan cost helper | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | `scanCostVer2`, line 841 |\n| Pre-cost path pruning | `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go` | `skylinePruning`, line 1119 |\n| Plan comparison | `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go` | `compareTaskCost`, line 349 |\n| Task enumeration | `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go` | `enumeratePhysicalPlans4Task`, line 172 |\n| DataSource best plan | `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go` | `findBestTask4DataSource` (inner loop), lines 1526\u20131588 |\n| Row-count for IndexScan | `pkg/planner/cardinality/row_count_index.go` | `GetRowCountByIndexRanges`, line 41 |\n| Stats struct | `pkg/statistics/table.go` | `HistColl` (Pseudo, RealtimeCount, ModifyCount) |\n| Stats derivation | `pkg/planner/core/stats.go` | `deriveStats4LogicalIndexScan` (line 92), `deriveStats4LogicalTableScan` (line 61) |\n| Version dispatch | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | `getPlanCost`, line 46 |\n",

Cost Calculation for IndexScan\n\n### Cost Model Version 1 (Ver1)\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go`\n**Function:** `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer1` (line 425)\n\nFormula:\n```\nselfCost = rowCount * rowSize * scanFactor\n```\n\n- `rowCount` \u2014 from `getCardinality(p, costFlag)`, which reads `p.StatsInfo().RowCount`\n- `rowSize` \u2014 from `p.getScanRowSize()`, average byte size of projected index columns\n- `scanFactor` \u2014 from `sessVars.GetScanFactor(p.Table)` (session var `tidb_opt_scan_factor`,\n  default 1.5); switches to `GetDescScanFactor` for descending scans larger than\n  `cost.SmallScanThreshold` (10 000 rows)\n\n### Cost Model Version 2 (Ver2)\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go`\n**Function:** `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer2` (line 123)\n\nFormula (via `scanCostVer2`, line 841):\n```\ncost = rows * max(log2(rowSize), 0) * scanFactor\n```\n\n- `rows` \u2014 `getCardinality(p, option.CostFlag)`\n- `rowSize` \u2014 `getAvgRowSize(p.StatsInfo(), p.schema.Columns)` (index columns only)\n- `scanFactor` \u2014 `getTaskScanFactorVer2(p, kv.TiKV, taskType)`\n\nThe `IndexReader` wrapper adds a network cost on top:\n```\nnetCost  = rows * rowSize * netFactor\nplanCost = (childCost + netCost) / distConcurrency\n```\n(`PhysicalIndexReader.GetPlanCostVer2`, line 216)\n\n---\n\n## 2. (curIsBetter bool, err error) {\n    curCost,  curInvalid,  err := getTaskPlanCost(curTask, ...)\n    bestCost, bestInvalid, err := getTaskPlanCost(bestTask, ...)\n    if curInvalid  { return false, nil }\n    if bestInvalid { return true,  nil }\n    return curCost < bestCost, nil\n}\n```\n\n`getTaskPlanCost` (line 370) dispatches to `getPlanCost`, which selects **Ver1** or **Ver2**\nbased on `CostModelVersion == modelVer2` (`plan_cost_ver2.go:47`).\n\n### Top-level Enumeration\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go`\n**Functions:** `findBestTask` (line 501), `enumeratePhysicalPlans4Task` (line 172)\n\n`enumeratePhysicalPlans4Task` iterates all physical plan candidates, calls\n`pp.Attach2Task(childTasks...)`, and keeps the minimum-cost task via `compareTaskCost`\n(line 246). Regression Hypothesis\n\n### Root Cause: Cost Model Version Change Combined with Stale Index Statistics\n\nThe cost formula for both scan types is:\n\n**Ver1:** `cost \u221d rowCount \u00d7 rowSize \u00d7 scanFactor`\n**Ver2:** `cost \u221d rowCount \u00d7 log2(rowSize) \u00d7 scanFactor`\n\n**Scenario:**\n\n1. A TiDB upgrade changes `tidb_cost_model_version` from 1 (default before v6.5) to 2\n   (default from v6.5 onward).\n\n2. Under Ver1, a table with **wide rows** (large `rowSize`) produced a large TableFullScan\n   cost, making the IndexScan clearly cheaper even with a moderate row-count estimate.\n\n3. Under Ver2, the cost uses `log2(rowSize)` instead of `rowSize`. For wide rows, this\n   compresses the cost difference dramatically:\n   - If `rowSize = 256` bytes, Ver1 weighs it as `256\u00d7`, Ver2 as `log2(256) = 8\u00d7`.\n   - A composite index covering many columns may have `rowSize \u2248 64`, giving\n     `log2(64) = 6\u00d7` \u2014 very close to the table's `8\u00d7`.\n   - The IndexScan's cost advantage nearly vanishes, and if its `rowCount` estimate is\n     even slightly overestimated (e.g., stale histogram after bulk DML), the optimizer\n     flips to TableFullScan.\n\n4. Stale index statistics (`ModifyCount >> RealtimeCount`) cause `IndexStatsIsInvalid`\n   to return `true` (`pkg/statistics/index.go:131`), reverting index selectivity to\n   pseudo estimates and inflating the IndexScan `rowCount`.\n\n**Key parameters that control the regression:**\n\n| Parameter | Default | Effect on regression |\n|---|---|---|\n| `tidb_cost_model_version` | 2 (since v6.5) | Switching 1\u21922 compresses row-size weight via log2, narrowing the cost gap |\n| `tidb_opt_scan_factor` | 1.5 | Applied equally to both scans; cannot alone flip the plan |\n| `tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan` | OFF | When OFF, no penalty is added to TableFullScan even for unreliable stats |\n| Stale `HistColl` (high `ModifyCount`) | \u2014 | Triggers pseudo index estimation, inflating IndexScan rowCount |\n\n**How to verify and fix:**\n1. Run `SHOW STATS_META WHERE table_name = 'your_table'` \u2014 check if `modify_count` is\n   large relative to `row_count`.\n2. Run `ANALYZE TABLE your_table` to refresh statistics.\n3. Use `EXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose' SELECT ...` to inspect `estRows` and `estCost` for each\n   plan node.\n4. If the regression is purely from the model version change, set\n   `SET tidb_cost_model_version = 1` as a temporary workaround, or set\n   `SET tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan = 1` to apply the range-scan penalty and push the\n   optimizer back toward the index.\n\n---\n\n## Summary of Key Files and Functions\n\n| Concern | File | Function / Line |\n|---|---|---|\n| IndexScan cost (Ver1) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` | `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer1`, line 425 |\n| TableFullScan cost (Ver1) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` | `(*PhysicalTableScan).GetPlanCostVer1`, line 400 |\n| IndexScan cost (Ver2) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer2`, line 123 |\n| TableFullScan cost (Ver2) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | `(*PhysicalTableScan).GetPlanCostVer2`, line 140 |\n| Scan cost helper (Ver2) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | `scanCostVer2`, line 841 |\n| Version dispatch | (curIsBetter bool, err error) {\n    curCost,  curInvalid,  err := getTaskPlanCost(curTask, ...)\n    bestCost, bestInvalid, err := getTaskPlanCost(bestTask, ...)\n    if curInvalid  { return false, nil }\n    if bestInvalid { return true,  nil }\n    return curCost < bestCost, nil\n}\n```\n\n`getTaskPlanCost` (line 370) dispatches to `getPlanCost`, which selects **Ver1** or **Ver2**\nbased on `CostModelVersion == modelVer2` (`plan_cost_ver2.go:47`).\n\n### Top-level Enumeration\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go`\n**Functions:** `findBestTask` (line 501), `enumeratePhysicalPlans4Task` (line 172)\n\n`enumeratePhysicalPlans4Task` iterates all physical plan candidates, calls\n`pp.Attach2Task(childTasks...)`, and keeps the minimum-cost task via `compareTaskCost`\n(line 246). The winner is stored via `p.StoreTask(prop, bestTask)`.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Cardinality / Row-Count Estimation\n\n### StatsInfo\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/stats.go`\nKey functions:\n- `deriveStats4LogicalTableScan` (line 61) \u2014 builds row-count for TableScan from\n  `deriveStatsByFilter`, using histogram and TopN data from `pkg/statistics/`\n- `deriveStats4LogicalIndexScan` (line 92) \u2014 equivalent for IndexScan, also calls\n  `deriveStatsByFilter`\n- `initStats` (line 492) \u2014 loads the `statistics.Table` (including `HistColl`) into\n  `ds.TableStats`\n\n### Cardinality Package\n\n**Files:** `pkg/planner/cardinality/`\n- `GetRowCountByIndexRanges` (`row_count_index.go:41`) \u2014 uses index histogram to estimate\n  rows matching a set of ranges\n- `GetRowCountByIntColumnRanges` / `GetRowCountByColumnRanges` \u2014 table-side equivalents\n- `GetAvgRowSize` / `GetIndexAvgRowSize` \u2014 byte-width estimates used in the scan cost formula\n\n### Statistics Structs\n\n**File:** `pkg/statistics/table.go`\nKey fields on `statistics.HistColl`:\n- `RealtimeCount` \u2014 live row count updated via DML feedback\n- `ModifyCount` \u2014 accumulated inserts/deletes since last ANALYZE\n- `Pseudo` \u2014 true when no real statistics exist (triggers pseudo estimation)\n\n---\n\n## 5. Regression Hypothesis\n\n### Root Cause: Cost Model Version Change Combined with Stale Index Statistics\n\nThe cost formula for both scan types is:\n\n**Ver1:** `cost \u221d rowCount \u00d7 rowSize \u00d7 scanFactor`\n**Ver2:** `cost \u221d rowCount \u00d7 log2(rowSize) \u00d7 scanFactor`\n\n**Scenario:**\n\n1. A TiDB upgrade changes `tidb_cost_model_version` from 1 (default before v6.5) to 2\n   (default from v6.5 onward).\n\n2. Under Ver1, a table with **wide rows** (large `rowSize`) produced a large TableFullScan\n   cost, making the IndexScan clearly cheaper even with a moderate row-count estimate.\n\n3. Under Ver2, the cost uses `log2(rowSize)` instead of `rowSize`. For wide rows, this\n   compresses the cost difference dramatically:\n   - If `rowSize = 256` bytes, Ver1 weighs it as `256\u00d7`, Ver2 as `log2(256) = 8\u00d7`.\n   - A composite index covering many columns may have `rowSize \u2248 64`, giving\n     `log2(64) = 6\u00d7` \u2014 very close to the table's `8\u00d7`.\n   - The IndexScan's cost advantage nearly vanishes, and if its `rowCount` estimate is\n     even slightly overestimated (e.g., stale histogram after bulk DML), the optimizer\n     flips to TableFullScan.\n\n4. Stale index statistics (`ModifyCount >> RealtimeCount`) cause `IndexStatsIsInvalid`\n   to return `true` (`pkg/statistics/index.go:131`), reverting index selectivity to\n   pseudo estimates and inflating the IndexScan `rowCount`.\n\n**Key parameters that control the regression:**\n\n| Parameter | Default | Effect on regression |\n|---|---|---|\n| `tidb_cost_model_version` | 2 (since v6.5) | Switching 1\u21922 compresses row-size weight via log2, narrowing the cost gap |\n| `tidb_opt_scan_factor` | 1.5 | Applied equally to both scans; cannot alone flip the plan |\n| `tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan` | OFF | When OFF, no penalty is added to TableFullScan even for unreliable stats |\n| Stale `HistColl` (high `ModifyCount`) | \u2014 | Triggers pseudo index estimation, inflating IndexScan rowCount |\n\n**How to verify and fix:**\n1. Run `SHOW STATS_META WHERE table_name = 'your_table'` \u2014 check if `modify_count` is\n   large relative to `row_count`.\n2. Run `ANALYZE TABLE your_table` to refresh statistics.\n3. Use `EXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose' SELECT ...` to inspect `estRows` and `estCost` for each\n   plan node.\n4. If the regression is purely from the model version change, set\n   `SET tidb_cost_model_version = 1` as a temporary workaround, or set\n   `SET tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan = 1` to apply the range-scan penalty and push the\n   optimizer back toward the index.\n\n---\n\n## Summary of Key Files and Functions\n\n| Concern | File | Function / Line |\n|---|---|---|\n| IndexScan cost (Ver1) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` | `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer1`, line 425 |\n| TableFullScan cost (Ver1) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` | `(*PhysicalTableScan).GetPlanCostVer1`, line 400 |\n| IndexScan cost (Ver2) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer2`, line 123 |\n| TableFullScan cost (Ver2) | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | # TiDB Cost-Based Optimizer: IndexScan vs TableFullScan Regression Analysis

## Overview

This report documents the cost model components in TiDB's query optimizer that govern
the choice between IndexScan and TableFullScan, and identifies how a parameter change
could cause a plan regression.

---

## 1. Cost Calculation for IndexScan

### Cost Model Version 1 (Ver1)

**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go`  
**Function:** `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer1` (line 425)

Formula:
```
selfCost = rowCount * rowSize * scanFactor
```

- `rowCount` — from `getCardinality(p, costFlag)`, which reads `p.StatsInfo().RowCount`
- `rowSize` — from `p.getScanRowSize()`, i.e., average byte size of projected index columns
- `scanFactor` — from `sessVars.GetScanFactor(p.Table)` (session var `tidb_opt_scan_factor`, default 1.5);
  switches to `GetDescScanFactor` for descending scans larger than `cost.SmallScanThreshold` (10 000 rows)

### Cost Model Version 2 (Ver2)

**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go`  
**Function:** `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer2` (line 123)

Formula (via `scanCostVer2`):
```
cost = rows * max(log2(rowSize), 0) * scanFactor
```

- `rows` — `getCardinality(p, option.CostFlag)`
- `rowSize` — `getAvgRowSize(p.StatsInfo(), p.schema.Columns)` (index columns only)
- `scanFactor` — from `getTaskScanFactorVer2(p, kv.TiKV, taskType)`

Helper: `scanCostVer2` (line 841) — enforces `rowSize >= 1` before applying log2.

The `IndexReader` wrapper adds a **network cost** on top:
```
netCost = rows * rowSize * netFactor
planCost = (childCost + netCost) / distConcurrency
```
(`PhysicalIndexReader.GetPlanCostVer2`, line 216)

---

# TiDB Cost-Based Optimizer: IndexScan vs TableFullScan Regression Analysis

## Overview

This report documents the cost model components in TiDB's query optimizer that govern
the choice between IndexScan and TableFullScan, and identifies how a parameter change
could cause a plan regression.

---

## 1. Cost Calculation for IndexScan

### Cost Model Version 1 (Ver1)

**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go`
**Function:** `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer1` (line 425)

Formula:
```
selfCost = rowCount * rowSize * scanFactor
```

- `rowCount` — from `getCardinality(p, costFlag)`, which reads `p.StatsInfo().RowCount`
- `rowSize` — from `p.getScanRowSize()`, average byte size of projected index columns
- `scanFactor` — from `sessVars.GetScanFactor(p.Table)` (session var `tidb_opt_scan_factor`,
  default 1.5); switches to `GetDescScanFactor` for descending scans larger than
  `cost.SmallScanThreshold` (10 000 rows)

### Cost Model Version 2 (Ver2)

**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go`
**Function:** `(*PhysicalIndexScan).GetPlanCostVer2` (line 123)

Formula (via `scanCostVer2`, line 841):
```
cost = rows * max(log2(rowSize), 0) * scanFactor
```

- `rows` — `getCardinality(p, option.CostFlag)`
- `rowSize` — `getAvgRowSize(p.StatsInfo(), p.schema.Columns)` (index columns only)
- `scanFactor` — `getTaskScanFactorVer2(p, kv.TiKV, taskType)`

The `IndexReader` wrapper adds a network cost on top:
